{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01YagHk7WoBJ6dbFVDT7zw4h","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I understand the diagnostics flow:\n\n1. **ExtHostDiagnostics** (`src/vs/workbench/api/common/extHostDiagnostics.ts`):\n   - Manages diagnostic collections\n   - When diagnostics change, it sends them via `$changeMany` to the main thread\n\n2. **MainThreadDiagnostics** (`src/vs/workbench/api/browser/mainThreadDiagnostics.ts`):\n   - Receives diagnostics from the extension host\n   - Updates the marker service \n   - Also listens to marker changes and forwards non-owned markers back to the extension host\n\n3. **MarkerService**:\n   - The central service that stores diagnostics as markers\n   - Other parts of VS Code (like the Problems panel) subscribe to marker changes\n\nThe issue is that when files change on disk (e.g., from a Git branch switch), there's no mechanism to:\n1.
